Chutes Too Narrow

INSIDER BASEBALL LEAGUE DAILY

Friday, July 18, 2003


A body believed to be that of government scientist Dr David Kelly is found in Oxfordshire - an inquiry is subsequently held into his death.

The Convention on the Future of Europe finishes its work and proposes the first European Constitution.

The Second Congo War concludes with 2-5 million deaths since 1998.
